The first manner is that you make three or four burns, aligning according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cautery as we have said before; and do not rush your hand onto the entire cautery, let the patient rest on his back; and another manner of cauterizing is that you heat up the cautery with two veins, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and lift the area where the mouse is located, or the patient's sore comes toward the left side, and raise the area according to the area you are lifting, according to the length of the body, and the cautery should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 After that, press the two inflamed nerves until the openings are pierced from the other side, and then pull out the cautery, so there will be four [openings]. If you see, cauterize all the nerves at three openings.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After treatment when pus has been discharged for a long time, this is what the other remedy before mentioned is worth.
de ydropisie	Of hydropisy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Cautery does not work on dropsy except in the manner which is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 When the treatment according to the methods we have mentioned in the divisions does not work, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the anus, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the bladder, and two behind the back near the spine, and one at the worst place; and let the cauteries be close to the thick part of the skin.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les .ij. ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After letting the fire cautery heal for a long time, do not neglect the care of the patient after the cautery; and healing would hasten, and the two intentions (healing and God's help) would be united.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The form of the cautery for the belly is like the key that we have shown before; and for the back it is olive-shaped, as it has been mentioned before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical and full of water, it should be cauterized on the back between the little finger and ring finger; and hold the hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not insert too deeply, otherwise the water would burst out forcefully, and let the cautery be shaped like this:
Aprés fai sus .ij. jambes .ij. cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After doing two cauteries on each leg with the tip of the knife; let one of the cauteries be behind the knee and the other outside the leg; and leave the cauteries above for a long time to heal, as the citrus juice is in it; after healing the other wounds that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the treatment
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai .i. grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et .iiij. cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout .i. cautere clavile subtil, et .ij. cauteres sus les hainches.	When the hernia of the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, while the digestive and retentive virtues that are in the stomach and intestine are obstructed, and cannot be cured by means of treatments; and you see the patient suffering greatly and of strong constitution, do this: make one large cautery on the stomach as described earlier, the cautery of the stomach, around the circumference; and four subtle cauteries around the abdomen, one subtle cautery each on the flanks.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, do cautery on the joint, and one cautery on each finger, and two small cauteries on the stomach in place of the large one, for the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	On the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 When the hemorrhoids are deep-rooted, one or more, and are old and full of thick cold and moist corrupted humors, and have been treated as we have said in the previous divisions, and it does not help if you perform cauterization: III on the spine of the back, that which is far away from the sacrum and gradually forms a triangle, and the cautery should be placed below the buttock; and if you think that his stomach is chilled and meat does not cook, and the face swells, then the large cauterization is performed on the stomach as previously stated, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with the entire cauterizing iron; and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After curing the limb until it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the flesh growth which is called "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble .i. raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou .ij., et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you apply althelul, heat the cautery which seems like a razor, and then place it entirely over the althelul-coated wound; leave your hand so that the cautery reaches the vein opening, thus burning the wound; do this once or twice, and if there is much of althelul, cauterize each time as we have said; afterwards, cure with herbs until they are healed; and if you cauterize a large cautery over blisters, it will provide more aid.
de plaie mal curee	of an improperly healed wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot tolerate incision or opening, as we will explain in its place, this illness occurs that can only be healed by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 If any abscess comes with pus and is enlarged and filled with corrupt moisture, you should pierce it with a subtle probe and ensure that you know exactly how far the probe goes in.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 After heating the cautery that resembles a razor, push it into the abscess according to how far the probe has entered, and repeat the cautery until the body burns and corrupts once or twice, as much as is needed; be careful not to burn the nerve or large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 If the abscess goes to the body of the bladder or intestines, be careful with those areas and not perform the cautery outside of the charred area, and consider that it is not persistent; after curing the limb until it is healthy, if the limb is pierced and materials have been removed for a long time, then know that the limb is healed completely; if the materials are not removed, then know that the limb is broken, and burn the bone at its base. And as one of us will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	Kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra .iij. cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When cold pain comes to the kidneys, accompanied by large swelling, and does not take on female form, then it requires cautery over the kidneys on both sides with the cautery described earlier; and if we cauterize it in the middle, it will have four cauteries in a line, and will provide more assistance.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et .i. a destre et .i. a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais .i. cautere defuers le dos, ou .ij. se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold or moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then make a cautery on the area outside of the bladder, where the pubic hair begins, one on the right side and one on the left, both as long as our thumb; and make one incision on the back, or two if necessary; and let the incisions be like the shape mentioned before.
de la marris	of the kidney
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice .iij. cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et .ij. cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the matrix is cold and moist and does not allow conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their terms delay; and when they come, they feel great pain: then it is necessary to apply four cauteries around the womb, as we have said (cautere of the bladder), and two cauteries behind the back; and may the cauteries be sharp, as we have said.
de la hainche	When the loins are cold and moist, and do not allow conception, and the seed is corrupted and its term prolonged; and when it comes, it causes great pain: then it is necessary to apply four cauteries around the flanks, as we have said (cautere of the bladder), and two cauteries behind the back; and may the cauteries be sharp, as we have said.
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a .i. cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous fluids descend into the belly of the loins, and because of this it moves away from its place, and the signs are that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the joints are found to be dislocated, if so you must cauterize the patient on the belly of the loins with one cautery resembling a circle, and sign in front of the joint around the belly so that the belly is within the circle; and may the cautery be like those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai .iij. cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this fire cautery is not present for you, make 4 large olive oil cauteries and let them be as perfect as all the others; and apply it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain from the hernia
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the area of the hernia, and it is caused by coldness and moisture; and the patient is cured with what has been said in the division, but the treatment is not effective, and the illness is old: then you must purge the patient from the thick humors using fetid pills or other good-seeming pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 After that, perform cauterization; and the method of cauterization is according to two methods: namely, with burning substances, and cauterization by fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 Cauterization by fire has many methods, one of which is to cauterize in the middle of the haunch three triangular cauteries according to this form, making a good depth and large incision, with space between each cautery the size of a thumb, and the cauteries should be olive-shaped; sometimes cauterization is made in the middle of the haunch on the head of the thigh, for which there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you wish, cauterize the cautery of the circle that we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the haunch, but make it so that the circles encompass the entire haunch, and all the fat surrounding it is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain persists in the hip, and does not reach as far as the thigh nor the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 If it reaches the thigh and the leg, have him perform fire cautery where he feels the pain, and make the incision 4 fingers above the ankle, to the left a little; let the cautery be a lancet, and let the thickness of the coal be as desired; and if he feels that the pain extends to two fingers or near there, have him cauterize where he feels the pain, 3 or 4 times at the location called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if necessary, do more; and if the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, make a fire cautery with a cutlery or circular cautery, and be very careful in all your cauteries not to let the cautery burn nerves and large arteries, and not to cause greater harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 And I myself have seen many who have performed fire cautery above the ankle and allowed it to remain until the leg was completely swollen, and the feet also, and all the toes were pierced and ruined.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a belly solution in which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 And if the pain is in two places together, make a cautery in one and in the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	 And say to the patient in the cautery of the incision, as follows, make such a knife and be its tip as thick as a fingernail of the thumb or slightly less, and be it between cuts or one between cut and the other with a space the size of a nutmeg; and let the cuts be above two parts, and let them be like nuts, and have the iron handle well made; and this is its shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois .i. cautere reont et lou laisse .iij. jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be scorched until it is all red and blistered, and then place it on the sick person's bed, turning it towards the healthy side; and cauterize once with one hot iron and leave it for 3 days; then make a plaster of butter, and keep the wound open for a long time; after that, treat it with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we should use this cautery sparingly due to fear of its appearance, and not many seem to use it; nevertheless, this is a good cautery for those who can endure it, and in places where it adheres.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 The medical cautery burning instrument is that you make it with cuts that penetrate the margin of the opening, and it should be made of iron or steel long enough, and at the top have two notches, and between each have the size of a thimble; and they should be turned over and above, and join together in this manner:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 After placing the hot iron (cautery) on the patient's shoulder lying on his left side, then your hand very near to the iron; afterwards pour water between the two circles of the hot iron which should be heated in fire at the tip; and leave it for an hour, let the patient endure the heat and burn from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 For it burns like fire; and when the burn has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and gently raise the shoulder from the water, and leave it for three days, apply butter until the blackness of the burn is removed; and leave it for three more days for pus to drain out; and this will be the final aid after the ointment treatment until he is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 And if the pain has spread to the thigh or the leg, make him lie on his side according to what you have done in the haystack; and this is the method of hot cautery, and I have written about it or treated it in the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take quicklime and hot live coal, as much of one as the other, and grind them together and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 or have a small hole covered except that the tip of a thorn can enter; and place one pot on top of the other well sealed, and put hot coal and lime and warm cautery powder on top until you have enough powder in your hand; and leave it like that until it settles down and becomes ash or pot boiling, then take all that ash, and pour it onto hot coals and lime as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	 And then if it [the shoulder] becomes extremely hot and is treated with various medical operations and fire cauterizations for other members, because it does the same work as fire, and if other medicines are administered that cauterize well the wound, such as wax, tallow, honey, and almond oil mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 Gailens tells us of a cure in which an honorable man was healed from the pain of the hernia and sciatica, and highly praises it, and says that no other cure was applied, and that he was cured within a week when this cure was performed, and he bathed himself as instructed below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And he says in this manner that you take green litharge and dry it, grind it very finely with a little fat, and place it on the hernia and on the thigh and leg where the pain is felt, and hold it there; then leave it for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 And then make it enter the bath until the body is slightly heated, and place it on a bed, and the pain will disappear entirely and become healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 And know that no one should use such fire cautery, unless after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 And Dioscorides says that when the vein sciatic is cauterized by goat's fat, it helps much; and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Take flax and beat it with old oil, and place it on the hole which is between the toe of the foot and the other one called foscile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 Afterwards take dry goat's fat and heat it until it is charcoal, and place it on the flax, and leave it until it is saturated; and repeat in this way, and do not stop doing so until you believe through sense that it reaches the hock, and that the pain is ceased; and this method of cautery is called "cautery of goat's fat".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or from striking or excessive bleeding, or from similar causes of cold matter spreading, none of these cases are worth cauterization except for that caused by infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne .v. cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai .iij. cauteres ou .iiij. au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	Afterward, the patient should be purged of foul pills or similar substances applied to the back where the pain is located, three lines marked with incense, and in each line 5 or more cauterizations depending on the potency and quantity that the patient can bear; and the cauterization should be done according to the cauterization called "poins"; and if you see, do 4 cauterizations or 3 according to the medium clavicle cauterization in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	Often, this disease comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have a narrow anus when they defecate, and fear; and you find in the lower spine of the back and in us the appearance that comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you intend to cure it, if you cauterize it with the cautery of that kind according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 The cautery enlarges each part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you wish, cauterize around the spine with the cautery pointed two or three lines, and let the points be close to one another.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After curing the joint until it is healthy as we have said, be careful not to apply cautery in a gibbosity that is on a nerve's spine.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	The pain of the joints is due to swellings which are present in every member of the body. When it comes in the feet (they call it podagry properly), and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauteries as follows: make the patient ready for the cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive oil-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary to prick the hip area, do it with the entire cautery that is claimed as "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 And if the pains come up to the knee and other joints, which happens frequently, apply cautery on each knee with three or four cauteries of the olive-shaped cautery on each part; and if you need more, do more, but don't hold your hand further than necessary for the core to be burnt.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains descend until the genitals and the back, administer the fire cautery as we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 And if the pains are in the hands, make punctures at the joints two inches apart; and if no pain remains at the fingers, make punctures over each joint and the skin of the hand; and if the pains come to the sides or to the shoulders, cauterize each part, and administer good care to the patient and think about medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you give good care and purge the phlegm, it will be healed with God's aid.
de la routure dou syfac	of the breaking of the saffron
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When swelling comes in anger and the boils descend into the eyes and it is suddenly occurring, if you see it when you want to cure it, you must not let him eat on that day; and he should use things that loosen his stomach, so that phlegm descends from his stomach. After that, make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to hold his elbow as long as the boils are protruding, and rearrange them to your fingers, and sign on top of the swelling over the bone of the wrist, and at all one sign that is similar to half a circle above the chest; then heat the cautery in the shape shown here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until it becomes white and gives off odor.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 Then, push the shoulders back into place; and have the assistant hold his hand so it does not return; and work the thighs on the patient, and put the cushion and sergeant under him on the thighs, and another one beneath the knee to hold the hands; then place the cautery over the spot with your entire hand, hold it straight and continue until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, try again until you reach the bone; be careful that the cauterized area does not boil as you perform the cauterization; and beware that the patient does not die or suffer harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cauterization, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And the cauterization of children should be subtle according to their size, and that of grown men should be according to their measure; after three days, cure the wound from the cauterization with butter until the burn is healed; afterwards, use other medications until it is healthy, and have the patient lie on his back for forty days so that the wound heals well; and it is necessary that his exudations are allowed to dry out, so that the boils do not protrude when he gets up to go into rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 After forty days, when he wants to get up, have a soft bandage made for him and apply it for another forty days; let him rest well, so that he does not work too much or eat and drink excessively, and speak too loudly; if he follows this instruction, he will be completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I will tell you hereafter about the treatment for amputation in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	From the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 When roundworms appear in other bellies and are recognized, and you see that they do not grow any further, then apply the cautery to them according to their size, and burn the third part of the body; after that, cure it as we have said; and no one of the old ones has said that it should be burned with the cautery at three angles according to this shape:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 but first mark the place where the worm is and make a line above it along the width of the worm, and another below it, and then place your hand on the entire heated cautery handle.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 But the early cauteries are lighter and quicker.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	From ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes in any limb, either from falling or being hurt, and that pain lasts for a long time and medicine does not help, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "poins", and the cautery should be according to the length of the limb, its smallness and frailty, and its virtue and location of twisting and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 If the first cautery is healed, that's good; if not, repeat the other cautery on the same limb because it often changes in the nearby member, which means you must perform the cauterizations until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	When mixing medicines, be careful to measure each ingredient accurately and mix them well, so as not to create an incorrect or ineffective remedy.
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 The sickness can sometimes be helped by cauterization with great aid, and the same illness that comes from the corruption of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 Can you see the patient to be cauterized, take care if the illness is at its beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, and neither boils nor remains, and you doubt that the corruption will affect the entire patient, then perform V cauteries on the head: lift the head toward me, and the other towards the forehead to the end of the hair; and II (two) above the II (two) horns, and I (one) behind the nape; and leave your hand so that the cautery reaches the bone, and so that the scabs come out from it so that the vapors of the gross humors can escape; and cauterize on the swelling according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et .i. cautere en som lou neis, et .ij. cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et .vj. cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et .i. grant sus la crupie et .i. autre delez, et .ij. sus les .ij. espaules; et .ij. sus les coutes, et .ij. sus les tendrons dou pis, et .i. sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et .i. autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et .i. autre sus lou foie.	And if the flesh is scattered everywhere; it is clearly rotten, you must cauterize with the cauteries that we have said, namely one cautery on the neck, two cauteries on the spine of the neck, six cauteries on the spine of the back, one large one on the crotch and another small one, two on each shoulder, two on the sides, two on the tendons of the feet, one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands; and beware of nerves that are above the last calcaneum, do not burn them; and sometimes a cautery is made on the bone of the thumb, and one other on the bone of the stomach, and one other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the more you do with the fire cautery, the more help it provides and benefits the patient; and know that the sick person does not feel pain from the cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And the cautery should be large or small according to the members and joints, as you will find in ways of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After treating the wound with wheat flour with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 When a swelling appears in any member and is treated with medicines, oils, plasters, but is not healed, then perform cauteries on the member according to its size and smallness of the member; and let the cautery be slightly penetrating into the flesh's thickness; then cure it with oil until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 And sometimes they make a fire cautery at the hand, foot, and back, at the nerve ending that makes the limb numb, and thus if the flesh is cut away; however, no one should interfere unless he is knowledgeable about the members and the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	If a worm falls into the eye, you must put the infected eye into vinegar to make it sleep for a while, and then take out the worm with tweezers; if the worm does not come out, you should apply oil of roses or camomile to the eye.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the illness called "albaras" appears and the devices of medicine are useless, then cauterize it with a deep cautery, according to the thickness of the flesh, until the white spot is removed, and the color changes; then cure it with flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, blood of cattle and blood of almonds, each one in equal parts; mix them all together, tie it up in a cloth, and apply it to the place until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When a boil begins to form and you wish to stop it, if you cauterize it using a round fire cautery around the circumference of the boil.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 However, the wise say that one should cauterize in the middle of the boil; however, this does not seem good to me, because I fear that it will become ulcerated and rotten, and I have seen it happen once before; a more appropriate thing is that it should be cauterized around, using the fire cautery called "circular", as we have mentioned in the discussion of cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	The swelling that cannot heal
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	 When someone has a disease called "adubelati", which delays healing due to its excess or because the patient is elderly and weak with little blood, or because of age; and you see it hastening to heal: then cauterize it with many small cauteries around it by pricking. After that, leave it as it is.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 When it hastens to heal.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you wish to pierce it with the entire cautery, heat the cautery as follows:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 And place your hand in the middle of that disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauteries have pierced the core, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels them leaving their course of purification clear.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After that, cure it until it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another kind of disease there is called "corroding," and it is nothing but the consumption of a limb, for it consumes the limbs as fire dries up dry things.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 If you see this disease in a place that can be treated with cautery along with fire, then heat the cauteries little and big, as needed for the place where the disease is; after cauterizing all around until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, remove everything that is corrupted.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then leave it for three days, and put on the affected areas softened cautery ground with oil until the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After the treatment of wounds producing pus.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 And if you see after three days that healthy pus does not emerge, it is good; and if not, continue the fire cautery on the corrupt parts of the body.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 And this burn is sometimes cured with hot medicines instead of fire cautery; but in any case, fire cautery is more helpful, and I have already said the cure for hot medicines in the section on hot diseases; take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	sore on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 It often happens that through the foot a disease called "cloth" arises according to our intention, and it is a swelling full of pus which inflames the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the cauterizations for this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 It is known as cauterization by fire and cauterization by hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 Cauterization by fire is when the patient's head is heated with a pencil-like iron, made of good iron that can pierce the nail from all sides and has narrow margins; then put it all hot over the nail, turn your hand around the nail until it comes out of the nail hole; leave it like this for three days until it starts to discharge pus; then make a plaster with bitter herbs ground with oil, and leave the plaster on top of it all night, and the nails will shrivel up and be removed from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal the joint with soothing ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 And if it is turned outside the body, and this happens in both hands and feet, you must apply hot cautery; and do it like this: take a cane of iron or copper, or a feather from the boar's bristle, and place it on top and the salve, that is to say to remove warts; and place the cane so that it surrounds completely, then put a little hot water there, and hold your hand well, and press your hand while turning so that the edge of the cane comes to the root of the nail, and may find the hot water penetrates deeply to the root; and let the patient endure for an hour a little bite of the hot water; then leave it, and it will be uprooted completely with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 Thus treat another, as long as you strengthen all those in the body, then heal the ones that are inflamed with warm ointments.
li cure dou trembler	the trembling cures
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices .iiij. cauteres ou .iv. sus l’espinee dou dos, .i. cautere entre chescune espinee; et .i. cautere ou pez, et .i. sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When someone shakes from cold or from quartan fever or another illness, you must make 4 or 5 fire cauterizations along the spine of the back, one between each vertebra; and 1 cauterization on the heel, and 1 on the stomach using the olive-oil cauterization; it will stop the trembling, and the health will improve from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of putrid boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 Sometimes, through the body, baths appear or pus-filled sores come, which come from large decayed substances.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 First, when they appear, it is necessary to perform a fire cauterization on each head of the pus-filled sore: a subtle cautery made from mirte wood, whose point should be immersed in fire, or a long root of arum lancifolium, or a cauterizing lentil.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear in this way, and they cannot grow further, but the excess from which they come is broken up, and they become healthy; however, it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Often there are large internal movements of blood from the cut artery at the wound, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cautery of a limb, and similar things; it is a very grave thing to let it out.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren .i., ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Nevertheless, whenever this happens, hasten to put your finger over the opening of the vein, and hold it very tightly so that the blood is stopped under your finger, and no more comes out; then take olive oil-soaked cotton balls of various sizes and apply them until they are all red; then take cotton made from hemp, or large or small according to the size of the wound and the location where the artery is damaged, and apply the cauterized cotton over the vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cauterized cotton in place until the blood is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the limb jumps violently when you place your hand on the vein, and the cautery is applied, take quickly another cautery that is near the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des .iiij. manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	Keep doing one after the other until the blood stops flowing; and be careful not to burn the nerve that is exposed, and ensure no further harm comes to the patient; and know that when the artery is large, it cannot be stopped from bleeding if not through one of the four ways we have mentioned: either by cautery, or extraction if it has not been treated, or by tightly tying a thread, or by medicines placed on it which can stop the blood; and bind and tighten it accordingly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever brings a tight binding of fabrics or places hot substances on it, or other similar things, if they do not help, will not benefit.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone who has no mirror or medicine present, you should place your finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it out until it is stretched taut over the wound and the vein; and do not move it, but moisten it with cold moisture often so that it becomes very cold until the blood is congealed and thickened and stretched taut; and inquire about the ones in front of whom you need cauteries and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical treatments
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases in which it is necessary to use fire cautery or hot medicines, and we have explained their types, causes, instruments, and forms of cauterization; and I placed that chapter from the head to the feet, and I will proceed in this chapter along the same path for those who seek it more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore, as I begin this, dear son, it is necessary that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for this reason, greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For many ways of people come in cures.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 Also come those who swear that they will die easily because of the foolishness they find in their disease and the great severity of their illness, and one should fear these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	 And among these there are those who give you advice and say: "Wait, I am cured"; but the disease is deceptive.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 It is not appropriate that you consent to those who come to you with this manner, but put more trust in your honor than in your desire, and do not be easily deceived but wisely of those from whom you are certain and whom you can rely on; and use diagnosis and guidance in the cures of your patients so that health may be converted; and this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dearest child, Our Lords grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration of His hand, come here.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have arranged this chapter in discussing by chapters, following the order of each chapter of cauteries that I have previously described to you from head to feet, as these are easier for you to understand what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The full head is swollen with water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	This disease often comes to children at childbirth, and sometimes it occurs due to an unknown reason.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and all those whom I have seen hurried death; and for this reason it seems to me that it is worthwhile to devote some treatment to certain cases.
Et je vis .i. enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com .ij. nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw one child whose head was swollen with water, and it grew larger every day until it could no longer support it; and the moisture gathered underneath the skull between the brain and the bone; and the treatment is such that if the moisture is between the brain and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you should make an incision large on the head; and let it be as long as two fingers, so that the moisture flows out; and see the shape of a lancet:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more swollen and the abscess is larger, make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief .iij. fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If the moisture is beneath the bone and you see the signs (of the abscess) as the corners of the head open up from each part, and the pus jumps out when you press it with your hand from within, and it does not heal: then you must make four incisions in the middle of the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 And after the incision remove all moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 And after the incision remove the bandages and powders, and put vinegar and oil on it, and leave it like that for five days; then unbind it, and heal the wound with stitches and ointments, and let the swelling subside gradually, and give the patient dry meat without moisture until the member is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	Another way of incision is that you look for the size of the abscess, and the flow of fluid; because sometimes it is in front, sometimes behind; sometimes on the right, and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Therefore, make the incision where the abscess opens, and empty the fluid, and do as you can; but be careful not to cover the artery; and let a vein of blood flow, so that the patient dies with dignity and from the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of gout
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it happens with any disease called "catarrh" in the eyes or at the worst, and the disease is old and medicine does not help at all, then the last cure is the cautery, namely by cutting two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 Therefore, when you wish to bind it, the patient should bend down; after that, rub the place with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then the patient should tightly fasten their neck with the cloth; then look where the veins are, and the places on either side of the ears are found; then mark the places to be cut, then cut one and the other with a sharp spatula of two fingers deep, so that the incision comes up to the bone, and this should be along the large part of the neck.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you want to cut them, push the spatula under the artery and cut it from above, while cutting as deep as 2 fingers through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when a vein is cut, it leaps out continually without stopping.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 If the artery does not open on its own, then you should measure the space of three feet and then drill to the bone; and the amount of blood that needs to be let out is 6 cubic centimeters, and sometimes a little more or less according to what the patient can bear, and the filling of the artery; then observe the wound: if it remains above the bone without swelling, then the pus from the abscess will not come, then hold the wound closed and tie it, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of immigration
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migration comes and an acute catarrh, due to moisture in the eyes, heat in the temples and an ancient madness, which seems like other things, and it is treated with methods of medicines, but none of them benefit, we should open the arteries of the temples and cauterize, as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is that the patient pulls the hairs on his temples, and listens to the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well with its beating, and is easily found except in some cold people; and if it is found, the patient should strain the neck with some cloths, then rub the place with a rough cloth, and burn the place with hot water until the artery appears clearly; then take the spatumile (a medical instrument) as shown here:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 Then lightly scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it up to the clamps, and remove carefully the threads that are underneath from each part; and if the artery is thin, then turn it at the point of the scissors, then tie off that section according to the amount of the two shoulders.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 If it is not cut (or injured), it cannot move at all by itself.
Et trai dou sanc des .vj. c/, jusc’a .iij.; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en .ij. leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les .ij. liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw out the blood from the .vj. c/, up to .iij.; and if the arteries are large, you must tie it with a double strong silk thread so that pus does not come before the wound is sealed, and there is drainage of blood; then cut off the excess between the .ij. ligaments at that same hour, and if possible, cauterize the area with a cautery knife up to the bone until the head is amputated; this is the mutilating work, if the patient does not have fever and has a hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	The cauteries are aid for healing wounds: therefore it is of greatest aid to those who are wounded.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de .ij. pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	It is necessary for the extraction of arteries that one fills the area with old cotton and places well-made tourniquets on it; and when they are loosened, one should be cured with dry medicines that produce heat, and tourniquets, until it is healed; and if without cutting the artery as you work, you must hasten to cover it by cauterizing, or use vitriol and hold it with your hand so that it is scorched; and if this is not present, place your thumb on the area until it freezes, and moisten the area with cold water until it stops, and hold as necessary; and the one that is mutilated and easier in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein of this sharp cautery twice, but the cuts should be wide enough to keep its heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the straw is too thin, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les .ij. coutelz .i. doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les .ij. leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en .ij. leus; et soient esloigniet entre les .ij. chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it should have between the two knives, one thickness of a finger's space, and then when you have signed up to a depth of two inches, and heat the iron hot enough for it to reach the bone, strike the vein in intervals of two inches; they should be spaced apart as they are not entirely sealed by this fire cautery, and this is the form of the cautery.
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears flow from the eyes that are above the vein on the forehead of the head, and it does not benefit the medicine applied to them, and you see the patient wrinkling his forehead like shivering; and if they are thin and moist so that the hair of the eyebrows falls out, and the eyebrows are burned and scorched by the heat of the tears, this treatment is required.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	 And it was called by the ancients "cure contused", and you should make at the back of the patient who has this disease let the hairs grow long, especially on the forehead; then you will make three cuts equally along the length of the forehead; one cut shall be as deep as necessary down to the bone below the eyebrows, and the other two shall pass through both cheeks above the eyelids, and be careful not to cut the arteries that are located above the eyelids; and distance your hand from the continuation of the lower jaws, and each wound should be the quantity of three fingers joined together; and prepare a piece of sponge and much cloth for sucking out the blood, then insert the sharp spatula made as shown in this figure:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les .ij. fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	from the first incision which is at the temple to the second incision; and scrape all the core that is between the two cuts to the root of the bone, then continue from the mid-incision to the other second one, and draw out this pointed spoon.
